3a2(myang 'das): tir gyur pa yod na/ do zhu zhing dri ba'i dus nang gi tha ma 'dir zhu zhing gsol cig/ ces pa'i gsung gis yongs su grags par gyur to// de'i tshe
3a3(myang 'das): bcom ldan 'das snga dro'i dus kyi tsha/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od rnam pa sna tshogs bkye ba ni/ 'di lta ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po dang / shal

3a5(myang 'das): gnas pa'i lam rgyud drug gi sems can dag/ 'od zer des reg ma thag tu kha na ma tho ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad byang bar gyur to// de'i tshe so so'i skye bo
3a6(myang 'das): dag de lta bu'i ltas mthong zhing thos nas mya ngan chen pos yid gdungs te/ dus gcig tu cho 'debs shing ngus nas 'di skad du/ e ma'o shin tu byams
3b1(myang 'das): pa'i pha mar gyur pa/ kyi hud kyi hud mya ngan las 'das sam zhes smras nas/ thal mos mgo dang brang la rdebs te che de rdung ngo // kha cig ni lus kyang rab tu 'dar zhing ba spu kun langs nas/ skad kyis brnangs
3b2(myang 'das): pa tsam du dus so/ / de'i tshe na sa chen po dang / ri dang / rgya mtsho yang rab tu g.yos shing 'khrugs so// de nas sems can de dag gcig la gcig spro bsring zhing mya ngan bsang ba'i phyir 'di
3b3(myang 'das): skad du/ kye grogs po dag mya ngan ma byed par myur du rtsa mchog gi grong khyer skyes bu stobs po che 'byung ba'i gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba der 'dong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i
3b4(myang 'das): zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ de bzhin gshegs pa yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' bar 'jig rten na bskal pa gcig gam/ bskal pa gcig 'grib kyi bar du bzhugs par gsol du
3b5(myang 'das): 'deng ngo zhes smras so/ / la la ni gcig gi lag pa la gcig gis 'jus nas 'di skad du/ 'jig rten stongs te sems can gyi bsod nams zad pas/ mi dge ba'i las 'jig rten
3b6(myang 'das): du 'byung bar gyur gyis/ grogs po dag de bzhin gshegs pa ni ring por mi thogs par yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar gshegs nges kyis/ bdag cag myur du 'deng ngo zhes smra'o//
3b7(myang 'das): la la ni 'di skad du 'jig rten stongs so// 'jig rten stongs so// bdag cag la deng slan chad ni mgon dang skyabs med de dbul 'phongs par gyur to// deng kho nar bla na med pa'i bcom ldan
4a1(myang 'das): 'dus dang yongs su bral bas/ da slan chad the tsom dang som nyi za ba su la zhu zhes smra'o// de'i tshe na tshad med pa'i nye gnas chen po tshe dang ldan pa
4a2(myang 'das): ka t+ya ya na chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa ba ku la dang / tshe dang ldan pa bsnyen dga' bo la sogs pa dge slong chen po de dag kyang / sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg pas lus kun
4a3(myang 'das): 'dar zhing mi bzod pa tsam du rab tu g.yos te/ sems kyang myos nas cho nges 'debs shing / de lta bu'i sdug bsngal rnam pa sna tshogs kyis non par gyur to//
4a4(myang 'das): de'i tshe gzhan yang dge slong brgya stong phrag brgyad cu snyed thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pa/ bya ba byas pa/ nyon mongs pa yongs su spangs pa/ dbang
4a5(myang 'das): po thams cad rab tu dul ba/ klu'i rgyal po chen po ltar mthu che ba/ stong pa'i shes rab dang ldan pa/ phyir bdag gi don rab tu rnyed pa tsan dan gyi tshal ltar tsan dan
4a6(myang 'das): gyis yongs su bskor ba/ seng ge'i rgyal po ltar seng ges yongs su bskor ba/ de lta bu'i tshad med pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi sras yang dag pa sha stag
4a7(myang 'das): gode dag kyang snga dro nya ma shar ma thag tu gnas nas byung ste/ so shing 'cha' ba na sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg nas/ gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ grogs po dag myur du
4b1(myang 'das): lag khrus shig ces smras so/ / de skad ces smras ma thag tu lus kyi ba spu kun langs nas lus la khyab par khrag gis rgyas pa ni me tog pa la sha lta bur gyur te/
4b2(myang 'das): mig mchi mas gang nas sdug bsngal chen po myong bar gyur to// de dag thams cad kyang sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i don gyi phyir/ theg pa chen po don dam pa stong pa nyid
4b3(myang 'das): la rnal 'byor du bsgrub pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pas thabs su dgongs te gsungs pa dag bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam pa sna tshogs su chos ston pa rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir/ sems
4b4(myang 'das): can thams cad yongs su gdul ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der myur du dong nas/ spyi bos sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong du bskor nas/
4b5(myang 'das): thal mo sbyar te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang ku ta la'i bu mo dge slong ma dpal bzangs dang / dge slong ma bsten dga' ma dang / dge slong ma rgya
4b6(myang 'das): mtsho'i blo gros la sogs te/ dge slong ma khri phrag drug cu snyed thams cad kyang dgra bcom pa/ zag pa zad pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pa/ bya ba byas pa/ nyon mongs pa
4b7(myang 'das): yongs su spangs pa/ dbang po rab tu dul ba/ klu chen po ltar gzi brjid rab tu che ba/ stong pa nyid kyi shes rab dang ldan pa sha stag ste/ de dag kyang snga dro'i dus kyi tshe nyi ma thog ma
5a1(myang 'das): shar ba na lus kyi ba spu kun skyi bung zhes byed nas/ lus la khyab par khrag gis rgyas pa ni me tog pa la sha lta bur gyur te/ mig mchi mas yongs su gang nas
5a2(myang 'das): sdug bsngal chen po myong bar gyur to/ / de dag kyang sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ theg pa chen po'i don dam pa'i stong pa nyid la rnal 'byor du bsgrub pa'i phyir/ de
5a3(myang 'das): bzhin gshegs pas thabs su dgongs te gsungs pa dag bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam pa sna tshogs su chos ston pa rgyan mi gcad pa'i phyir/ sems can thams cad yongs su gdul ba'i phyir/
5a4(myang 'das): bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der myur du dong nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor nas/ thal mo sbyar te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do//
5a5(myang 'das): dge slong ma de dag gi nang na dge slong ma kha cig ni byang chub sems dpa' ste/ mi'i nang na klu lta bu sa bcu rab tu non pa/ mi g.yo ba la gnas pa/ sems can gdul ba'i phyir bud
5a6(myang 'das): med kyi lus ston kyang rtag tu tshad med pa bzhi la nan tan byed pa/ sems kyi dbang du gyur pas sangs rgyas kyi skur yang sprul pa sha stag go// de'i tshe gzhan yang krung
5a7(myang 'das): gang+gA gcig gi bye ma snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i mi'i nang na klu lta bu sa bcu rab tu non pa/ mi g.yo ba la rab tu gnas pa/ thabs kyis lus ston pa sha stag la
5b1(myang 'das): 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' blo gros mi zad pa la sogs te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gis thog mar drangs

5b3(myang 'das): chen po la shin tu srung ba/ 'jig rten du bcas pa thams cad kyi sems dang spor ba/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su ma grol ba grel bar yi dam 'cha' ba/ 'das pa'i dus na bskal pa grangs
5b4(myang 'das): med pa'i bar du tshul khrims yongs su bsrungs pa/ spyod pa yongs su 'dzin pa/ ma grol ba grol bar byed pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad par 'tshob pa/ ma
5b5(myang 'das): 'ongs pa'i dus su chos kyi 'khor lo skor bar 'gyur pa/ rgyan chen pos shin tu brgyan pa/ de lta bu'i yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la bu gcig pa dang
5b6(myang 'das): 'dra bar lta ba sha stag go/ / de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma shar ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyis reg ma thag tu lus kyi ba spu kun langs te/ lus la khyab par khrag gis rgyas pa ni ji

7a1(myang 'das): shing tsan dan dang / a ka ru dang / 'go shir sha tsan dan dang / lha'i shing bsung can la sogs pa'o// shing de dag kyang mdzes pa'i ri mo dang ldan zhing / rin po che

7b1(myang 'das): mdun na rin po che sna bdun gyi rgyal mtshan lnga bcu snyed mngar te/ gser gyi dra bas bla rer bres so// shing rta de re re'i steng yang rin po che'i gdugs lnga bcu snyed bres so// shing rta re re re la yang me tog gi

9b3(myang 'das): pa/ lus 'di la khyi ro dang 'dra bar 'jigs su rung ba dang / lus 'di ni mi gtsang ba ste/ bu ga dgu nas rtag tu zag par rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni mkhar dang 'dra ste/ sha dang / pags

29a7(myang 'das): lus mi rtag pa'i lus so/ / sbyin pa phyis bzhes pa ni nyon mongs pa ma mchis pa'i sku/ rdo rje lta bu'i chos kyi sku/ rtag pa'i sku/ mtha' yas pa'i sku lags na/ ci'i slad du sbyin pa rnam
29b1(myang 'das): pa gnyis kyi 'bras bu khyad par ma mchis zhes gsungs/ sngar sbyin pa blangs pa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par mi 'gyur ba nas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du
29b2(myang 'das): rdzogs par mi 'gyur te/ sha'i mig 'ba' zhig thob kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan ma thob pa nas/ shes rab kyi spyan gyi bar du thob pa ma lags so// sbyin pa phyis bzhes pa ni sbyin pa'i
29b3(myang 'das): pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pa nas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du yongs su rdzogs la/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan dang ldan pas na/ shes rab kyi spyan gyi bar du ldan pa
29b4(myang 'das): lags na/ ci'i slad du sbyin pa rnam pa gnyis kyi 'bras bu khyad par ma mchis zhes gsungs/ bcom ldan 'das sbyin pa sngar blangs pa ni blangs ma thag tu 'tshal nas/ de ma thag tu
29b5(myang 'das): zhu bas tshe dang / mdog dang / stobs dang / bde ba dang / so sor yang dag par shes pa thob pa lags so// sbyin pa phyis bzhes pa ni gsol ba dang zhu ba'ang ma mchis la/ 'bras
29b6(myang 'das): bu rnam pa lnga po'ang ma mchis na/ ci'i slad du sbyin pa rnam pa gnyis kyi 'bras bu khyad par ma mchis zhes gsungs// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs
29b7(myang 'das): kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa ni bskal pa tshad med mtha' yas grangs med pa'i bar du/ zas sam nyon mongs pa dang bcas pa'i sku ma yin/ nang gi tha ma'i sku ma yin te/ rtag pa'i sku/

30a7(myang 'das): sngon de bzhin gshegs pas gnag rdzi me ran ta dang / nan ta pa la gnyis kyis 'o ma'i 'jam phul ba bzhes nas/ gdod tha ma med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par

30b6(myang 'das): rgyas 'jig rten du gshegs pa yang shin tu rnyed dka' la/ sangs rgyas dang phrad nas dad pa skyed pa yang shin tu dka'/ chos thos pa yang shin tu dka'/ sangs rgyas yongs su mya
30b7(myang 'das): ngan las 'das kar mchod pa bshams te phul ba shin tu dka'o/ / tsun da la phyag 'tshal lo// khyod ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs te/ ston gyi chos bco lnga'i zla ba

31a6(myang 'das): skyes bu khyu mchog ni/ / yongs su mya ngan 'da' zhes gsungs// bdag cag rnams la snying rje phyir// sangs rgyas bzhugs par gsol ba thob// yun du 'jig rten 'dir bzhugs
31a7(myang 'das): shing / / tshad med 'khor la phan pa'i phyir// mkhas pa rnams kyis bsngags pa yi// tha med chos mchog bshad du gsol// khyod kyis gsol ba ma btab na// bdag cag
31b1(myang 'das): rnams ni mi 'tsho'o/ / de bas khyod kyis gsol ba thob// kha lo sgyur ba'i ston pa la// de'i tshe tsun da shin tu dga' mgu rangs pa ni/ dper na mi zhig pa ma shi ba las

31b3(myang 'das): du gyur/ / mi yi lus kyang legs par thob// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug bsal// ngan song gsum yang yongs su spangs// legs so bde ba'i don gyur te// rin chen gser
31b4(myang 'das): gyi ri mthong nas/ / ston pa kha lo sgyur dang mjal// byol song khams su skye mi dogs// sangs rgyas u dum war ltar// phrad pa'i dus kyang shin tu dka'// phrad nas dge

32a1(myang 'das): chen po'i nang / / rus sbal long ba 'byung ba de// shing gi bu gar mgo chung bzhin// sangs rgyas 'byung ba de bas dka'// bdag gis mchod pa gsol

32a3(myang 'das): re/ / ci ste thob par gyur na yang // de la dga' ba mos pa med// bcom ldan bdag gi mchod pazhes pas// shin tu dga' ba dpag ma mchis// e ran da yi me tog la//

206b2(myang 'das): gsung ngo snyam sems te/ so so nas bdag 'ba' zhig gi khyim du gshegs te/ bdag 'ba' zhig gi mchod pa bzhis so snyam sems so// sems can la la ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i tshad med par rgya chen
206b3(myang 'das): por mthong ngo / / la la ni sku rab tu chung ngur mthong ngo // la la ni nyan thos kyi gzugs lta bur mthong ngo // la la ni rang sangs rgyas kyi gzugs lta bur mthong ngo // mu stegs can kha cig ni 'di snyam du de ba

206b5(myang 'das): de bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin yang dag pa ni zla ba dang 'dra ste/ chos kyi sku/ mi skye ba'i sku/ thabs kyi sku ste/ 'jig rten pa'i rjes su sngon gyi las rnam pa tshad med pa/ gnas thams cad du skye ba bstan pa ni zla/

207a1(myang 'das): lag pa bskum pa na 'jigs rten pa dag ni zla ba phyir skyes so zhes zer te/ zla ba 'di ni sdug bsngal yang myong ngo zhes zer ro// gal te lha ma yin brgya stong snyed tshogs kyang zla ba la ni

342a1(myang 'das): dag pa ste/ sems can tshad med pa la phan pa dang bde ba'i don du gyur pa/ ma rig pa'i mun pa chen por chos chen po'i sgron ma snang bar byed pa/ bdag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos chen po bsrung zhing
342a2(myang 'das): bskyab pa'i phyir khyod kyis sems 'khrugs shing gnod pa byas pa dag 'gyod cing 'thol lo/ / khyod ni ma 'ongs pa'i dus su nges par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par 'tshang rgya ba na/ bdag cag kyang
342a3(myang 'das): bsgral bar smon to/ / de'i tshe brgya byin lha'i dbang phyug dang / lha'i sras po rnams byang chub sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal nas mi snang bar gyur to// rigs kyi bu nga sngon tshigs su bcad pa byed kyi phyir yang lus yongs su btang
342a4(myang 'das): ste de'i rgyu de'i rkyen gyis bskal pa bcu gnyis kyis byams pa bas/ sngar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas so// rigs kyi bu ngas de ltar tshad med pa'i yon tan thob pa'ang de bzhin
342a5(myang 'das): gshegs pa'i yang dag pa'i chos la mchod pa'i dbang gis so/ / rigs kyi bu khyod kyang de dang 'dra ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' tshad med mtha
342a6(myang 'das): yas pa klung kang+gA'i bye ma snyed pas shin tu 'phags te phul du gyur to/ / rigs kyi bu de lta na byang chub sems dpa' theg pa chen po yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa la gnas pa na/ 'phags pa'i spyad pa
